### [105] [From Agent Loops to Structured Graphs:A Scheduler-Theoretic Framework for LLM Agent Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11378)
*Hu Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出SGH（结构化图框架）作为替代传统Agent Loop的新范式，将控制流从隐式上下文提升为显式静态DAG，以解决Agent Loop的三个结构弱点


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Agent Loop存在三个结构弱点：步骤间的隐式依赖、无界恢复循环、以及使调试复杂化的可变执行历史。当前基于LLM的代理构建范式需要更可控、可验证和可实现的替代方案

Method: 提出SGH框架，包含三个核心承诺：执行计划在计划版本内不可变；将规划、执行和恢复分离为三层；恢复遵循严格的升级协议。采用静态DAG结构，将控制流显式化

Result: 这是一个立场论文和设计提案，提供了理论框架、设计分析和实验协议，但没有生产实现或实证结果。贡献包括：调度器统一框架、70个系统的权衡分析、形式化规范、以及可归因的实验框架

Conclusion: SGH通过牺牲一些表达能力来换取可控性、可验证性和可实现性，将Agent Loop和图执行引擎置于统一的语义连续体上，为LLM代理执行提供了更结构化的替代方案

Abstract: The dominant paradigm for building LLM based agents is the Agent Loop, an iterative cycle where a single language model decides what to do next by reading an ever growing context window. This paradigm has three structural weaknesses: implicit dependencies between steps, unbounded recovery loops, and mutable execution history that complicates debugging. We characterize the Agent Loop as a single ready unit scheduler: at any moment, at most one executable unit is active, and the choice of which unit to activate comes from opaque LLM inference rather than an inspectable policy. This perspective places Agent Loops and graph based execution engines on a single semantic continuum. We propose SGH, Structured Graph Harness, which lifts control flow from implicit context into an explicit static DAG. SGH makes three commitments: execution plans are immutable within a plan version, planning execution and recovery are separated into three layers, and recovery follows a strict escalation protocol. These choices trade some expressiveness for controllability, verifiability, and implementability. Our contributions are fourfold: a scheduler unified framework that applies classical scheduling theory to LLM agent execution and identifies challenges introduced by non deterministic LLM nodes; a trade off analysis of controllability, expressiveness, and implementability across 70 surveyed systems; a formal specification including a node state machine with termination and soundness guarantees; and an attributable experimental framework with a seven group design for future validation. This is a position paper and design proposal. We provide a theoretical framework, design analysis, and experimental protocol, not a production implementation or empirical results.

</details>


### [106] [Three Roles, One Model: Role Orchestration at Inference Time to Close the Performance Gap Between Small and Large Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11465)
*S. Aaron McClendon,Jorge Gallego-Feliciano,Stavros Zervoudakis,Antonios Saravanos*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 通过推理时脚手架技术，在不增加训练计算的情况下，显著提升小模型在复杂多步环境中的性能，使8B模型超越33B模型的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型代理在现实工具使用任务中表现良好，但在有限硬件上部署能力强的代理仍然具有挑战性。研究是否仅通过推理时脚手架（无需额外训练计算）就能提升小模型在复杂多步环境中的性能。

Method: 提出三层次推理脚手架管道：1) 总结模型：压缩对话历史同时保留关键信息；2) 主要代理模型：在压缩上下文中进行推理；3) 独立校正模型：审查和修订代理的代码输出，打破重复失败循环。所有角色使用相同的冻结模型权重。

Result: 脚手架技术使Qwen3-8B模型性能翻倍：FP16配置从5.4%提升到8.9%，AWQ配置从3.0%提升到5.9%。在难度1任务上提升尤为显著。FP16推理中，脚手架化的8B模型超越了DeepSeek-Coder 33B Instruct的7.1%性能。

Conclusion: 结构化推理时干预可以使小模型在性能上媲美大4倍的模型，证明了推理时计算扩展的价值。该方法被形式化为基于冻结基础模型的脚手架策略，为强化学习中的动作空间塑造提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents show promise on realistic tool-use tasks, but deploying capable agents on modest hardware remains challenging. We study whether inference-time scaffolding alone, without any additional training compute, can improve the performance of a small model in complex multi-step environments. Operating on a single 24\,GB GPU, we evaluate Qwen3-8B under both full-precision (FP16, 12K context) and 4-bit quantized (AWQ, 32K context) configurations. Without any intervention, the raw model achieves just 5.4\% (FP16) and 3.0\% (AWQ) task goal completion. Guided by a systematic failure mode analysis, we introduce a three-tier inference scaffolding pipeline that deploys the same frozen model in three distinct roles: (1) a summarization model that preserves critical artifacts (tokens, credentials, API responses) while compressing dialogue history; (2) the main agent model that reasons over the compressed context; and (3) an isolated correction model that reviews and revises the agent's code output without access to conversation history, breaking repetitive failure loops. Applied to the same unmodified model, this scaffolding yields 8.9\% (FP16) and 5.9\% (AWQ) task goal completion, roughly doubling performance in both settings, with particularly strong gains on difficulty-1 tasks (15.8\%$\to$26.3\% FP16; 5.3\%$\to$14.0\% AWQ). On full-precision inference, our scaffolded 8B model surpasses DeepSeek-Coder 33B Instruct (7.1\%) from the original AppWorld evaluation, demonstrating that structured inference-time interventions can make small models competitive with systems 4$\times$ their size. We formalize the approach as a scaffolded policy over a frozen base model, three invocations of the same weights with different conditioning, drawing connections to test-time compute scaling and action-space shaping in reinforcement learning.

</details>


### [107] [PAC-BENCH: Evaluating Multi-Agent Collaboration under Privacy Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11523)
*Minjun Park,Donghyun Kim,Hyeonjong Ju,Seungwon Lim,Dongwook Choi,Taeyoon Kwon,Minju Kim,Jinyoung Yeo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着专用AI智能体越来越多地部署并与其他智能体交互协作，但隐私约束下的多智能体协作动态机制仍未被充分理解，需要系统性的评估框架

Method: 提出PAC-Bench基准测试，用于系统评估隐私约束下的多智能体协作，通过实验分析隐私约束对协作性能的影响

Result: 隐私约束显著降低协作性能，使结果更依赖于发起智能体而非合作伙伴；分析发现性能下降主要由早期隐私违规、过度保守抽象和隐私诱导幻觉等协调崩溃导致

Conclusion: 隐私感知的多智能体协作是一个独特且未解决的挑战，需要超越现有智能体能力的新协调机制

Abstract: We are entering an era in which individuals and organizations increasingly deploy dedicated AI agents that interact and collaborate with other agents. However, the dynamics of multi-agent collaboration under privacy constraints remain poorly understood. In this work, we present $PAC\text{-}Bench$, a benchmark for systematic evaluation of multi-agent collaboration under privacy constraints. Experiments on $PAC\text{-}Bench$ show that privacy constraints substantially degrade collaboration performance and make outcomes depend more on the initiating agent than the partner. Further analysis reveals that this degradation is driven by recurring coordination breakdowns, including early-stage privacy violations, overly conservative abstraction, and privacy-induced hallucinations. Together, our findings identify privacy-aware multi-agent collaboration as a distinct and unresolved challenge that requires new coordination mechanisms beyond existing agent capabilities.

</details>


### [108] [Problem Reductions at Scale: Agentic Integration of Computationally Hard Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11535)
*Xi-Wei Pan,Shi-Wen An,Jin-Guo Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 利用AI编码代理构建大规模问题归约库，通过工程化约束、验证系统和反馈循环，在3个月内创建了包含100+问题类型和200+归约规则的Rust库


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决NP难优化问题时，需要针对特定求解器（量子硬件、商业优化器或领域启发式方法）重新表述问题。构建一个通用的多项式时间归约库可以让用户通过单一接口将任何支持的问题路由到任何支持的求解器，但大规模构建这样的库一直难以实现。

Method: 采用"harness engineering"方法，设计约束、验证系统和反馈循环来引导AI编码代理。包括：为领域专家提供无代码贡献途径；多层验证栈（从类型级检查到代理特征测试，即AI代理扮演最终用户角色）；全自动的实现-评审-集成流水线。

Result: 在约3个月内，构建了一个命令行工具，支持包含100+问题类型和200+归约规则的库，代码量超过17万行Rust代码。新的求解器注册到任何单个问题类型后，通过归约路径连接的每个问题都能立即使用该求解器。

Conclusion: 精心设计的工程化约束可以让AI代理以超越先前归约库努力的规模和速度构建经过良好测试的软件。归约图的传递组合性使得新求解器能够快速扩展到整个问题网络。

Abstract: Solving an NP-hard optimization problem often requires reformulating it for a specific solver -- quantum hardware, a commercial optimizer, or a domain heuristic. A tool for polynomial-time reductions between hard problems would let practitioners route any supported problem to any supported solver through a single interface. Building such a library at scale, however, has remained out of reach. We show that harness engineering, the practice of designing constraints, verification systems, and feedback loops that channel AI coding agents, can overcome this barrier. Our harness combines a no-code contribution route for domain experts, a multilayer verification stack ranging from type-level checks to agentic feature tests (AI agents role-playing as end users), and a fully automated implementation-review-integration pipeline. In about three months, we built a command-line tool backed by a library of 100+ problem types and 200+~reduction rules in over 170k lines of Rust. The result suggests that a well-engineered harness lets agents build well-tested software at a scale and pace beyond prior reduction-library efforts. Because the reduction graph composes transitively, a new solver registered for any single problem type instantly becomes available to every problem connected by a reduction path. The source code is available at https://github.com/CodingThrust/problem-reductions.

</details>

Method: 采用双模型协作架构：Mat-R1（30B参数）作为分析模型提供领域专家级推理，Mat-T1（14B参数）作为执行模型协调工具操作。通过熵分析确认该架构解决了工具规划和分析推理之间的冲突。

Abstract: Current large language models require hundreds of billions of parameters yet struggle with domain-specific reasoning and tool coordination in materials science. Here, we present MatBrain, a lightweight collaborative agent system with two synergistic models specialization for crystal materials research. MatBrain employs a dual-model architecture: Mat-R1 (30B parameters) as the analytical model providing expert-level domain reasoning, and Mat-T1 (14B parameters) as the executive model orchestrating tool-based actions. Entropy analysis confirms that this architecture resolves the conflict between tool planning and analytical reasoning by decoupling their distinct entropy dynamics. Enabled by this dual-model architecture and structural efficiency, MatBrain significantly outperforms larger general-purpose models while reducing the hardware deployment barrier by over 95%. MatBrain exhibits versatility across structure generation, property prediction, and synthesis planning tasks. Applied to catalyst design, MatBrain generated 30,000 candidate structures and identified 38 promising materials within 48 hours, achieving approximately 100-fold acceleration over traditional approaches. These results demonstrate the potential of lightweight collaborative intelligence for advancing materials research capabilities.

As model capabilities converge, this harness layer is becoming the primary site of architectural differentiation. Second is the evolution of human-agent interaction from discrete tasks toward a persistent, contextually aware collaborative relationship, which demands open, trustworthy and extensible harness infrastructure. We present SemaClaw, an open-source multi-agent application framework that addresses these shifts by taking a step towards general-purpose personal AI agents through harness engineering. Our primary contributions include a DAG-based two-phase hybrid agent team orchestration method, a PermissionBridge behavioral safety system, a three-tier context management architecture, and an agentic wiki skill for automated personal knowledge base construction.

*Yijuan Liang,Xinghao Chen,Yifan Ge,Ziyi Wu,Hao Wu,Changyu Zeng,Wei Xing,Xiaoyu Shen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: UniToolCall是一个统一的工具学习框架，通过标准化工具集构建、数据集生成和评估流程，显著提升LLM工具使用能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究存在交互表示不一致、忽视工具使用轨迹结构分布、评估基准不兼容等问题，需要统一的工具学习框架。

Method: 构建包含22k+工具的大型工具池，创建390k+实例的混合训练语料，引入Anchor Linkage机制支持多轮推理，将7个公共基准转换为统一的QAOA表示。

Abstract: Tool-use capability is a fundamental component of LLM agents, enabling them to interact with external systems through structured function calls. However, existing research exhibits inconsistent interaction representations, largely overlooks the structural distribution of tool-use trajectories, and relies on incompatible evaluation benchmarks. We present UniToolCall, a unified framework for tool learning that standardizes the entire pipeline from toolset construction and dataset generation to evaluation. The framework curates a large tool pool of 22k+ tools and constructs a hybrid training corpus of 390k+ instances by combining 10 standardized public datasets with structurally controlled synthetic trajectories. It explicitly models diverse interaction patterns, including single-hop vs. multi-hop and single-turn vs. multi-turn, while capturing both serial and parallel execution structures. To support coherent multi-turn reasoning, we further introduce an Anchor Linkage mechanism that enforces cross-turn dependencies. Furthermore, we convert 7 public benchmarks into a unified Query--Action--Observation--Answer (QAOA) representation with fine-grained evaluation at the function-call, turn, and conversation levels. Experiments show that fine-tuning Qwen3-8B on our dataset substantially improves tool-use performance. Under the distractor-heavy Hybrid-20 setting, achieves 93.0% single-turn Strict Precision, outperforming commercial models including GPT, Gemini, and Claude.

### [112] [RationalRewards: Reasoning Rewards Scale Visual Generation Both Training and Test Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11626)
*Haozhe Wang,Cong Wei,Weiming Ren,Jiaming Liu,Fangzhen Lin,Wenhu Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出RationalRewards模型，通过结构化推理将人类偏好转化为多维度的解释性评价，在训练时提供细粒度强化学习奖励，在测试时通过生成-评价-优化循环改进输出，无需参数更新。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉生成的奖励模型通常将丰富的人类判断简化为单一分数，丢弃了偏好背后的推理过程。这限制了奖励模型作为主动优化工具的能力。

Method: 提出PARROT框架，通过锚定生成、一致性过滤和蒸馏，从现成的偏好数据中恢复高质量的解释性评价。训练RationalRewards模型（8B参数），使其能产生明确的多维度评价后再进行评分。

Result: RationalRewards在开源奖励模型中达到最先进的偏好预测性能，与Gemini-2.5-Pro竞争，但训练数据量减少10-20倍。作为强化学习奖励，在文本到图像和图像编辑任务上优于标量替代方案。测试时的评价-优化循环在多个基准上匹配或超过基于强化学习的微调。

Conclusion: 结构化推理能够解锁现有生成器中潜在的能力，这些能力在次优提示下无法被激发。将奖励模型从被动评估者转变为主动优化工具，通过解释性评价提供更有效的训练和测试时优化。

Abstract: Most reward models for visual generation reduce rich human judgments to a single unexplained score, discarding the reasoning that underlies preference. We show that teaching reward models to produce explicit, multi-dimensional critiques before scoring transforms them from passive evaluators into active optimization tools, improving generators in two complementary ways: at training time, structured rationales provide interpretable, fine-grained rewards for reinforcement learning; at test time, a Generate-Critique-Refine loop turns critiques into targeted prompt revisions that improve outputs without any parameter updates. To train such a reward model without costly rationale annotations, we introduce Preference-Anchored Rationalization (PARROT), a principled framework that recovers high-quality rationales from readily available preference data through anchored generation, consistency filtering, and distillation. The resulting model, RationalRewards (8B), achieves state-of-the-art preference prediction among open-source reward models, competitive with Gemini-2.5-Pro, while using 10-20x less training data than comparable baselines. As an RL reward, it consistently improves text-to-image and image-editing generators beyond scalar alternatives. Most strikingly, its test-time critique-and-refine loop matches or exceeds RL-based fine-tuning on several benchmarks, suggesting that structured reasoning can unlock latent capabilities in existing generators that suboptimal prompts fail to elicit.

### [114] [SWE-AGILE: A Software Agent Framework for Efficiently Managing Dynamic Reasoning Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11716)
*Shuquan Lian,Juncheng Liu,Yazhe Chen,Yuhong Chen,Hui Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SWE-AGILE提出了一种动态推理上下文策略，通过维护详细推理的滑动窗口和压缩历史推理摘要，解决了软件工程代理中推理深度与上下文限制的平衡问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的ReAct风格软件工程代理缺乏显式的System-2推理能力来处理复杂边缘情况。在SWE任务中，保留完整推理历史会导致上下文爆炸和"迷失在中间"问题，而丢弃历史又会迫使代理在每个步骤中冗余重新推理。

Method: SWE-AGILE引入了动态推理上下文策略：1) 维护详细推理的滑动窗口以保持即时连续性；2) 将历史推理内容压缩为简洁的推理摘要；3) 平衡推理深度、效率和上下文约束。

Result: 在SWE-Bench-Verified基准测试中，SWE-AGILE为7B-8B模型设定了新标准，仅使用2.2k轨迹和896个任务就取得了优异表现。

Conclusion: SWE-AGILE通过创新的动态推理上下文策略，成功解决了软件工程代理中推理深度与上下文限制之间的根本困境，实现了更高效的自主软件工程。

Abstract: Prior representative ReAct-style approaches in autonomous Software Engineering (SWE) typically lack the explicit System-2 reasoning required for deep analysis and handling complex edge cases. While recent reasoning models demonstrate the potential of extended Chain-of-Thought (CoT), applying them to the multi-turn SWE task creates a fundamental dilemma: retaining full reasoning history leads to context explosion and ``Lost-in-the-Middle'' degradation, while discarding it would force the agent to redundantly re-reason at every step. To address these challenges, we propose SWE-AGILE, a novel software agent framework designed to bridge the gap between reasoning depth, efficiency, and context constraints. SWE-AGILE introduces a Dynamic Reasoning Context strategy, maintaining a ``sliding window'' of detailed reasoning for immediate continuity to prevent redundant re-analyzing, while compressing historical reasoning content into concise Reasoning Digests. Empirically, SWE-AGILE sets a new standard for 7B-8B models on SWE-Bench-Verified using only 2.2k trajectories and 896 tasks. Code is available at https://github.com/KDEGroup/SWE-AGILE.

### [115] [Detecting Safety Violations Across Many Agent Traces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11806)
*Adam Stein,Davis Brown,Hamed Hassani,Mayur Naik,Eric Wong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Meerkat是一个结合聚类与智能搜索的系统，用于在大量智能体轨迹中检测自然语言描述的安全违规行为，相比现有方法显著提升了违规检测效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在检测安全违规时面临挑战：单轨迹分析会错过跨轨迹才可见的违规，智能审计难以扩展到大规模轨迹集合，固定监控器对未预期行为脆弱。这些问题在滥用活动、隐蔽破坏、奖励黑客攻击和提示注入等场景中普遍存在。

Method: Meerkat结合聚类与智能搜索：通过结构化搜索和自适应调查有希望的区域，无需依赖种子场景、固定工作流或穷举枚举。系统使用自然语言描述违规行为，在大量智能体轨迹中高效发现稀疏的违规。

Result: 在滥用、错位和任务博弈设置中，Meerkat显著优于基线监控器；在一个顶级智能体基准测试中发现了广泛的开发者作弊行为；在CyBench上发现的奖励黑客攻击示例比先前审计多近4倍。

Conclusion: Meerkat通过结合聚类与智能搜索的方法，有效解决了在大规模智能体轨迹中检测稀疏、复杂安全违规的挑战，为安全审计提供了可扩展且自适应的解决方案。

Abstract: To identify safety violations, auditors often search over large sets of agent traces. This search is difficult because failures are often rare, complex, and sometimes even adversarially hidden and only detectable when multiple traces are analyzed together. These challenges arise in diverse settings such as misuse campaigns, covert sabotage, reward hacking, and prompt injection. Existing approaches struggle here for several reasons. Per-trace judges miss failures that only become visible across traces, naive agentic auditing does not scale to large trace collections, and fixed monitors are brittle to unanticipated behaviors. We introduce Meerkat, which combines clustering with agentic search to uncover violations specified in natural language. Through structured search and adaptive investigation of promising regions, Meerkat finds sparse failures without relying on seed scenarios, fixed workflows, or exhaustive enumeration. Across misuse, misalignment, and task gaming settings, Meerkat significantly improves detection of safety violations over baseline monitors, discovers widespread developer cheating on a top agent benchmark, and finds nearly 4x more examples of reward hacking on CyBench than previous audits.

</details>


### [116] [Collaborative Multi-Agent Scripts Generation for Enhancing Imperfect-Information Reasoning in Murder Mystery Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11741)
*Keyang Zhong,Junlin Xie,Hefeng Wu,Haofeng Li,Guanbin Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一个协作多智能体框架，用于评估和合成高质量的角色驱动多人游戏剧本，通过两阶段智能体监督训练策略提升视觉语言模型在复杂多跳推理和欺骗性信息下的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉语言模型在感知任务中表现出色，但在多人游戏设置中面对不完美和欺骗性信息时，复杂多跳推理能力会下降。需要解决在不确定、对抗性和社会复杂条件下训练和评估VLMs的挑战。

Method: 提出协作多智能体框架生成角色驱动的多人游戏剧本，包含角色背景、视觉和文本线索、多跳推理链。采用两阶段智能体监督训练策略：1) 基于思维链的微调，使用建模不确定性和欺骗性的数据集；2) GRPO强化学习，通过智能体监督的奖励塑形鼓励角色特定推理行为。

Result: 实验表明该方法显著提升了VLMs在叙事推理、隐藏事实提取和欺骗弹性理解方面的性能，为在不确定、对抗性和社会复杂条件下训练和评估VLMs提供了可扩展解决方案。

Conclusion: 该方法为在不确定、对抗性和社会复杂条件下训练和评估VLMs提供了可扩展解决方案，为多模态多跳推理在不完美信息下的未来基准测试奠定了基础。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) have shown impressive capabilities in perceptual tasks, yet they degrade in complex multi-hop reasoning under multiplayer game settings with imperfect and deceptive information. In this paper, we study a representative multiplayer task, Murder Mystery Games, which require inferring hidden truths based on partial clues provided by roles with different intentions. To address this challenge, we propose a collaborative multi-agent framework for evaluating and synthesizing high-quality, role-driven multiplayer game scripts, enabling fine-grained interaction patterns tailored to character identities (i.e., murderer vs. innocent). Our system generates rich multimodal contexts, including character backstories, visual and textual clues, and multi-hop reasoning chains, through coordinated agent interactions. We design a two-stage agent-monitored training strategy to enhance the reasoning ability of VLMs: (1) chain-of-thought based fine-tuning on curated and synthetic datasets that model uncertainty and deception; (2) GRPO-based reinforcement learning with agent-monitored reward shaping, encouraging the model to develop character-specific reasoning behaviors and effective multimodal multi-hop inference. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method significantly boosts the performance of VLMs in narrative reasoning, hidden fact extraction, and deception-resilient understanding. Our contributions offer a scalable solution for training and evaluating VLMs under uncertain, adversarial, and socially complex conditions, laying the groundwork for future benchmarks in multimodal multi-hop reasoning under imperfect information.

</details>

### [117] [Building an Internal Coding Agent at Zup: Lessons and Open Questions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09805)
*Gustavo Pinto,Pedro Eduardo de Paula Naves,Ana Paula Camargo,Marselle Silva*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: Zup公司开发的CodeGen内部编码代理表明，工具设计、安全护栏和渐进式人工监督等工程决策比模型本身更能决定编码代理的实际价值


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业团队在构建内部编码代理时面临原型性能与生产就绪性之间的差距，技术模型质量不足以确保实际应用成功，需要关注工具设计、安全执行、状态管理和人工信任校准等工程因素

Method: 开发CodeGen内部编码代理，采用针对性工具设计（如字符串替换编辑而非完整文件重写）、分层安全护栏，以及渐进式人工监督模式来驱动有机采用

Result: 目标工具设计和分层安全护栏比提示工程更能提高代理可靠性，渐进式人工监督模式促进了有机采用而无需强制信任

Conclusion: 围绕模型的工程决策（而非模型本身）决定了编码代理在实践中是否能提供真正价值

Abstract: Enterprise teams building internal coding agents face a gap between prototype performance and production readiness. The root cause is that technical model quality alone is insufficient -- tool design, safety enforcement, state management, and human trust calibration are equally decisive, yet underreported in the literature. We present CodeGen, an internal coding agent at Zup, and show that targeted tool design (e.g., string-replacement edits over full-file rewrites) and layered safety guardrails improved agent reliability more than prompt engineering, while progressive human oversight modes drove organic adoption without mandating trust. These findings suggest that the engineering decisions surrounding the model -- not the model itself -- determine whether a coding agent delivers real value in practice.

</details>


### [118] [Automating Structural Analysis Across Multiple Software Platforms Using Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09866)
*Ziheng Geng,Jiachen Liu,Ian Franklin,Ran Cao,Dan M. Frangopol,Minghui Cheng*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 开发了能够跨多个结构分析软件平台（ETABS、SAP2000、OpenSees）自动化框架结构分析的大语言模型，采用两阶段多智能体架构，实现超过90%的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注让LLM操作单一结构分析软件平台，但实际工程中结构工程师经常依赖多种有限元分析工具（如ETABS、SAP2000、OpenSees），这限制了LLM辅助工程工作流的实际部署。

Method: 采用两阶段多智能体架构：第一阶段，多个智能体协作解释用户输入并进行结构化推理，推断几何、材料、边界和荷载信息，输出统一的JSON表示；第二阶段，代码翻译智能体并行工作，将JSON文件转换为多个结构分析平台的可执行脚本，每个智能体都针对目标软件的语法规则和建模工作流程进行提示。

Result: 使用20个代表性框架问题在三个广泛使用的平台（ETABS、SAP2000、OpenSees）上评估LLM，十次重复试验结果显示性能稳定可靠，所有案例准确率超过90%。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了能够跨多个软件平台自动化结构分析的LLM，解决了现有研究的局限性，为实际工程部署提供了可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have shown the promise to significantly accelerate the workflow by automating structural modeling and analysis. However, existing studies primarily focus on enabling LLMs to operate a single structural analysis software platform. In practice, structural engineers often rely on multiple finite element analysis (FEA) tools, such as ETABS, SAP2000, and OpenSees, depending on project needs, user preferences, and company constraints. This limitation restricts the practical deployment of LLM-assisted engineering workflows. To address this gap, this study develops LLMs capable of automating frame structural analysis across multiple software platforms. The LLMs adopt a two-stage multi-agent architecture. In Stage 1, a cohort of agents collaboratively interpret user input and perform structured reasoning to infer geometric, material, boundary, and load information required for finite element modeling. The outputs of these agents are compiled into a unified JSON representation. In Stage 2, code translation agents operate in parallel to convert the JSON file into executable scripts across multiple structural analysis platforms. Each agent is prompted with the syntax rules and modeling workflows of its target software. The LLMs are evaluated using 20 representative frame problems across three widely used platforms: ETABS, SAP2000, and OpenSees. Results from ten repeated trials demonstrate consistently reliable performance, achieving accuracy exceeding 90% across all cases.

</details>


### [119] [MR-Coupler: Automated Metamorphic Test Generation via Functional Coupling Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10126)
*Congying Xu,Hengcheng Zhu,Songqiang Chen,Jiarong Wu,Valerio Terragni,Shing-Chi Cheung*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: MR-Coupler利用方法间的功能耦合关系自动构建蜕变关系和生成蜕变测试用例，显著提高了蜕变测试的自动化程度和有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蜕变测试虽然能缓解测试预言问题，但构建有效的蜕变关系需要领域专业知识，阻碍了其实际应用。需要自动化方法来降低构建难度。

Method: 识别功能耦合的方法对，使用大语言模型生成候选测试用例，通过测试扩增和变异分析进行验证。利用三种功能耦合特征减少方法对枚举，采用新颖验证机制降低误报。

Result: 在100个人工编写的测试用例和50个真实bug上评估，MR-Coupler为超过90%的任务生成有效测试用例，有效测试生成提升64.90%，误报降低36.56%，检测到44%的真实bug。

Conclusion: 功能耦合是自动化构建蜕变关系的有效方法，MR-Coupler有潜力促进蜕变测试的实际应用。已开源工具和实验数据支持后续研究。

Abstract: Metamorphic testing (MT) is a widely recognized technique for alleviating the oracle problem in software testing. However, its adoption is hindered by the difficulty of constructing effective metamorphic relations (MRs), which often require domain-specific or hard-to-obtain knowledge. In this work, we propose a novel approach that leverages the functional coupling between methods, which is readily available in source code, to automatically construct MRs and generate metamorphic test cases (MTCs). Our technique, MR-Coupler, identifies functionally coupled method pairs, employs large language models to generate candidate MTCs, and validates them through test amplification and mutation analysis. In particular, we leverage three functional coupling features to avoid expensive enumeration of possible method pairs, and a novel validation mechanism to reduce false alarms. Our evaluation of MR-Coupler on 100 human-written MTCs and 50 real-world bugs shows that it generates valid MTCs for over 90% of tasks, improves valid MTC generation by 64.90%, and reduces false alarms by 36.56% compared to baselines. Furthermore, the MTCs generated by MR-Coupler detect 44% of the real bugs. Our results highlight the effectiveness of leveraging functional coupling for automated MR construction and the potential of MR-Coupler to facilitate the adoption of MT in practice. We also released the tool and experimental data to support future research.

</details>

*Ragib Shahariar Ayon*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该博士研究提出系统研究多智能体LLM结对编程，通过外部化意图和使用开发工具进行迭代验证，旨在提高代码生成的可信度、可审计性和可维护性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于LLM的编码智能体虽然能生成代码、测试和文档，但输出可能看似合理却与开发者意图不符，且在演进项目中缺乏足够的审查证据。这限制了我们对如何构建LLM结对编程工作流的理解，以确保工件随时间保持可靠、可审计和可维护。

Method: 提出三个研究：1) 将非正式问题陈述转化为符合标准的需求和形式化规范；2) 使用自动反馈（如求解器支持的反例）精炼测试和实现；3) 支持维护任务（重构、API迁移、文档更新）同时保留已验证行为。

Result: 预期成果包括：更清晰理解多智能体工作流何时能增加信任，以及为构建可靠编程助手提供实用指导。

Abstract: LLM-based coding agents are increasingly used to generate code, tests, and documentation. Still, their outputs can be plausible yet misaligned with developer intent and provide limited evidence for review in evolving projects. This limits our understanding of how to structure LLM pair-programming workflows so that artifacts remain reliable, auditable, and maintainable over time. To address this gap, this doctoral research proposes a systematic study of multi-agent LLM pair programming that externalizes intent and uses development tools for iterative validation. The plan includes three studies: translating informal problem statements into standards aligned requirements and formal specifications; refining tests and implementations using automated feedback, such as solver-backed counterexamples; and supporting maintenance tasks, including refactoring, API migrations, and documentation updates, while preserving validated behavior. The expected outcome is a clearer understanding of when multi-agent workflows increase trust, along with practical guidance for building reliable programming assistants for real-world development.

### [121] [AdverMCTS: Combating Pseudo-Correctness in Code Generation via Adversarial Monte Carlo Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10449)
*Qingyao Li,Weiwen Liu,Weinan Zhang,Yong Yu,Bo An*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: AdverMCTS：一种对抗性蒙特卡洛树搜索框架，通过将代码搜索与主动漏洞发现相结合来对抗伪正确性，显著提升代码生成的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的代码生成方法依赖静态稀疏的公共测试用例进行验证，导致伪正确性问题——解决方案过度拟合可见的公共测试，但无法泛化到隐藏测试用例。固定、弱环境的优化本质上限制了鲁棒性。

Method: 提出AdverMCTS框架，将代码生成建模为极小极大博弈：Solver代理合成代码候选，Attacker代理进化生成针对性边界测试用例来利用当前代码池中的逻辑分歧。这些发现的测试形成动态、渐进敌对的过滤器来惩罚脆弱推理。

Result: 大量实验表明AdverMCTS显著优于现有最先进基线，有效降低误报率，并迫使模型泛化到初始约束之外。

Conclusion: 通过将代码搜索与主动漏洞发现相结合，AdverMCTS成功解决了伪正确性问题，提升了代码生成的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Abstract: Recent advancements in Large Language Models (LLMs) have successfully employed search-based strategies to enhance code generation. However, existing methods typically rely on static, sparse public test cases for verification, leading to pseudo-correctness -- where solutions overfit the visible public tests but fail to generalize to hidden test cases. We argue that optimizing against a fixed, weak environment inherently limits robustness. To address this, we propose AdverMCTS, a novel adversarial Monte Carlo Tree Search framework that combats pseudo-correctness by coupling code search with active vulnerability discovery. AdverMCTS formulates generation as a minimax-style game between a Solver agent, which synthesizes code candidates, and an Attacker agent, which evolves to generate targeted corner test cases that exploit logical divergences in the current code pool. These discovered tests form a dynamic, progressively hostile filter that penalizes fragile reasoning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AdverMCTS significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, effectively reducing false positive rates and forcing the model to generalize beyond the initial constraints. The resources of this work are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/AdverMCTS_open-A255.

</details>


### [122] [SWE-Shepherd: Advancing PRMs for Reinforcing Code Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10493)
*Mahir Labib Dihan,Md Ashrafur Rahman Khan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SWE-Shepherd框架通过过程奖励模型为代码智能体提供密集的步骤级监督，提高仓库级代码任务的交互效率和动作质量


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在处理真实软件工程任务时面临挑战：需要长时程推理、处理大型演化代码库、跨依赖动作做一致决策。现有方法依赖静态提示或手工启发式选择动作，缺乏对中间决策的细粒度反馈，导致探索效率低、错误传播和脆弱解决方案轨迹。

Method: 提出SWE-Shepherd框架，引入过程奖励模型为仓库级代码智能体提供密集的步骤级监督。使用SWE-Bench轨迹构建动作级奖励数据集，在基础LLM上训练轻量级奖励模型来估计中间动作的有用性。在推理时，PRM评估候选动作并引导智能体做出更高奖励的决策，无需完整强化学习。

Result: 在SWE-Bench Verified上的实验表明，该方法提高了交互效率和动作质量，同时也揭示了中间奖励与最终任务成功对齐的挑战。

Conclusion: SWE-Shepherd通过过程奖励模型为代码智能体提供密集监督，改善了仓库级软件工程任务的性能，但中间奖励与最终成功对齐仍需进一步研究。

Abstract: Automating real-world software engineering tasks remains challenging for large language model (LLM)-based agents due to the need for long-horizon reasoning over large, evolving codebases and making consistent decisions across interdependent actions. Existing approaches typically rely on static prompting strategies or handcrafted heuristics to select actions such as code editing, file navigation, and test execution, but they lack fine-grained feedback on intermediate decisions. This leads to inefficient exploration, error propagation, and brittle solution trajectories. To address this limitation, we propose SWE-Shepherd, a framework that introduces Process Reward Models (PRMs) to provide dense, step-level supervision for repository-level code agents. Using trajectories from SWE-Bench, we construct an action-level reward dataset and train a lightweight reward model on a base LLM to estimate the usefulness of intermediate actions. During inference, the PRM evaluates candidate actions and guides the agent toward higher-reward decisions without requiring full reinforcement learning. Experiments on SWE-Bench Verified demonstrate improved interaction efficiency and action quality, while also highlighting challenges in aligning intermediate rewards with final task success.

</details>


### [123] [How Many Tries Does It Take? Iterative Self-Repair in LLM Code Generation Across Model Scales and Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10508)
*Johin Johny Arimbur*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究评估了七种大语言模型在代码生成任务中的迭代自我修复能力，发现自我修复能显著提升代码通过率，其中Gemini 2.5 Flash表现最佳，断言错误最难修复，而现代指令调优模型仅通过提示就能成功进行自我修复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在首次尝试时经常无法生成正确的代码，但大多数基准测试都在单次尝试设置下评估它们。本研究旨在探索迭代自我修复（将执行错误反馈给模型进行修正）在不同模型上的效果，以了解现代模型在代码生成任务中的自我修复能力。

Method: 在HumanEval（164个问题）和MBPP Sanitized（257个问题）两个代码生成基准上，对七种模型进行最多五次尝试的迭代自我修复测试。模型包括Llama系列、Qwen3和Gemini系列，涵盖不同规模和架构（密集和MoE）。分析错误类型修复率，进行提示消融实验，比较自我修复与重新采样的权衡。

Result: 自我修复在所有模型上都显著提高了通过率：HumanEval上提升4.9-17.1个百分点，MBPP上提升16.0-30.0个百分点。Gemini 2.5 Flash达到最高最终通过率（HumanEval 96.3%，MBPP 93.8%）。大部分增益集中在前两轮。断言错误最难修复（约45%修复率），语法和名称错误修复率更高。现代指令调优模型仅通过提示就能成功进行自我修复，即使是8B规模的模型。

Conclusion: 迭代自我修复能显著提升大语言模型的代码生成性能，现代指令调优模型仅通过提示就能有效进行自我修复。断言错误是最难修复的错误类型，而链式思维修复提示能带来额外增益。研究还首次比较了密集和MoE架构在自我修复任务上的表现。

Abstract: Large language models frequently fail to produce correct code on their first attempt, yet most benchmarks evaluate them in a single-shot setting. We investigate iterative self-repair (feeding execution errors back to the model for correction) across seven models spanning three families and both open-weight and proprietary providers: Llama 3.1 8B, Llama 3.3 70B, Llama 4 Scout (MoE, 16 experts), Llama 4 Maverick (MoE, 128 experts), Qwen3 32B, Gemini 2.5 Flash, and Gemini 2.5 Pro. On HumanEval (164 problems) and MBPP Sanitized (257 problems) with up to five attempts, self-repair universally improves pass rates: +4.9 to +17.1 pp on HumanEval and +16.0 to +30.0 pp on MBPP. Gemini 2.5 Flash achieves the highest final pass rates (96.3% HumanEval, 93.8% MBPP). Most gains concentrate in the first two rounds.Error-type analysis shows assertion errors (logical mistakes) are the hardest to repair at ~45%, while syntax and name errors are repaired at substantially higher rates, connecting to broader findings on the limits of LLM self-correction. Prior work found that weaker models fail at self-repair or require fine-tuning; we show that modern instruction-tuned models succeed with prompting alone, even at 8B scale. We also provide the first comparison of dense and MoE architectures for self-repair, and extend the repair-vs-resampling tradeoff analysis to modern models. A prompt ablation reveals chain-of-thought repair yields up to +5.5 pp additional self-repair gain (measured as improvement in repair delta) over minimal prompting for capable models.

</details>

### [126] [VulWeaver: Weaving Broken Semantics for Grounded Vulnerability Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10767)

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: VulWeaver是一个基于LLM的漏洞检测方法，通过构建增强的统一依赖图、提取完整漏洞上下文，并采用元提示和多数投票机制，显著提升了漏洞检测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统静态分析工具构建的程序表示不准确，现有LLM方法缺乏关键漏洞上下文和基于事实的推理能力，导致漏洞检测效果有限。

Method: 1) 结合确定性规则和LLM语义推理构建增强统一依赖图；2) 通过程序切片提取显式上下文，结合使用、定义、声明等隐式上下文；3) 使用元提示和漏洞类型特定专家指南引导LLM系统推理，通过多数投票聚合结果。

Result: 在PrimeVul4J数据集上F1-score达到0.75，比最先进的学习型、LLM型和智能体基线分别提升23%、15%和60%；在9个真实Java项目中检测到26个真实漏洞，其中15个被开发者确认，5个获得CVE标识；在工业部署中发现40个已确认漏洞。

Conclusion: VulWeaver通过整合程序语义、提取完整上下文和系统化推理，显著提升了LLM在漏洞检测中的准确性和实用性，在实际应用中表现出色。

Abstract: Detecting vulnerabilities in source code remains critical yet challenging, as conventional static analysis tools construct inaccurate program representations, while existing LLM-based approaches often miss essential vulnerability context and lack grounded reasoning. To mitigate these challenges, we introduce VulWeaver, a novel LLM-based approach that weaves broken program semantics into accurate representations and extracts holistic vulnerability context for grounded vulnerability detection. Specifically, VulWeaver first constructs an enhanced unified dependency graph (UDG) by integrating deterministic rules with LLM-based semantic inference to address static analysis inaccuracies. It then extracts holistic vulnerability context by combining explicit contexts from program slicing with implicit contexts, including usage, definition, and declaration information. Finally, VulWeaver employs meta-prompting with vulnerability type specific expert guidelines to steer LLMs through systematic reasoning, aggregated via majority voting for robustness. Extensive experiments on PrimeVul4J dataset have demonstrated that VulWeaver achieves a F1-score of 0.75, outperforming state-of-the-art learning-based, LLM-based, and agent-based baselines by 23%, 15%, and 60% in F1-score, respectively. VulWeaver has also detected 26 true vulnerabilities across 9 realworld Java projects, with 15 confirmed by developers and 5 CVE identifiers assigned. In industrial deployment, VulWeaver identified 40 confirmed vulnerabilities in an internal repository.

### [127] [Verify Before You Fix: Agentic Execution Grounding for Trustworthy Cross-Language Code Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.10800)
*Jugal Gajjar*

Main category: cs.SE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统学习分类器在智能体管道中存在可靠性问题：概率性预测而非验证结论，未经执行验证就采取修复动作会导致下游阶段错误累积。软件漏洞分析使这一问题成本具体可测量。

Method: 构建统一的跨语言漏洞生命周期框架，包含三个LLM驱动的推理阶段：混合结构语义检测、执行验证的智能体验证、验证感知的迭代修复。采用通用抽象语法树（uAST）将Java、Python、C++标准化为共享结构模式，结合GraphSAGE和Qwen2.5-Coder-1.5B嵌入的混合融合，通过学习的双向门控机制实现内在可解释性。

Abstract: Learned classifiers deployed in agentic pipelines face a fundamental reliability problem: predictions are probabilistic inferences, not verified conclusions, and acting on them without grounding in observable evidence leads to compounding failures across downstream stages. Software vulnerability analysis makes this cost concrete and measurable. We address this through a unified cross-language vulnerability lifecycle framework built around three LLM-driven reasoning stages-hybrid structural-semantic detection, execution-grounded agentic validation, and validation-aware iterative repair-governed by a strict invariant: no repair action is taken without execution-based confirmation of exploitability. Cross-language generalization is achieved via a Universal Abstract Syntax Tree (uAST) normalizing Java, Python, and C++ into a shared structural schema, combined with a hybrid fusion of GraphSAGE and Qwen2.5-Coder-1.5B embeddings through learned two-way gating, whose per-sample weights provide intrinsic explainability at no additional cost. The framework achieves 89.84-92.02% intra-language detection accuracy and 74.43-80.12% zero-shot cross-language F1, resolving 69.74% of vulnerabilities end-to-end at a 12.27% total failure rate. Ablations establish necessity: removing uAST degrades cross-language F1 by 23.42%, while disabling validation increases unnecessary repairs by 131.7%. These results demonstrate that execution-grounded closed-loop reasoning is a principled and practically deployable mechanism for trustworthy LLM-driven agentic AI.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM编码代理使用MCP等工具协议在开发者工作站上读写文件时，当写入失败（由于内容过滤器、截断或会话中断），代理通常接收不到结构化信号，丢失草稿，并浪费token盲目重试。

Method: 提出Resilient Write MCP服务器，在代理和文件系统之间插入六层持久写入表面：预检风险评估、事务性原子写入、恢复安全分块、结构化类型错误、带外暂存存储、任务连续性移交信封。每层对应实际观察到的具体故障模式。

Conclusion: Resilient Write通过六层正交且可独立采用的持久写入表面，有效解决LLM编码代理写入失败问题，显著提高代理的恢复能力和自校正能力。

Abstract: LLM-powered coding agents increasingly rely on tool-use protocols such as the Model Context Protocol~(MCP) to read and write files on a developer's workstation. When a write fails -- due to content filters, truncation, or an interrupted session -- the agent typically receives no structured signal, loses the draft, and wastes tokens retrying blindly. We present \textbf{Resilient Write}, an MCP server that interposes a six-layer durable write surface between the agent and the filesystem. The layers -- pre-flight risk scoring, transactional atomic writes, resume-safe chunking, structured typed errors, out-of-band scratchpad storage, and task-continuity handoff envelopes -- are orthogonal and independently adoptable. Each layer maps to a concrete failure mode observed during a real agent session in April~2026, in which content-safety filters silently rejected a draft containing redacted API-key prefixes. Three additional tools -- chunk preview, format-aware validation, and journal analytics -- emerged from using the system to compose this paper. A 186-test suite validates correctness at each layer, and quantitative comparison against naive and defensive baselines shows a 5x reduction in recovery time and a 13x improvement in agent self-correction rate. Resilient Write is open-source under the MIT license.

To address this challenge, we present Sema Code, an open AI coding framework built on the principle of being embeddable, pluggable, and framework-first. Sema Code completely decouples the core agent engine from all client layers, publishing it as a standalone npm library that any runtime can drive programmatically. Built around this architecture, we designed eight key mechanisms: multi-tenant engine isolation, FIFO input queuing with safe session reconstruction, adaptive context compression, multi-agent collaborative scheduling, intelligent Todo-based process management, four-layer asynchronous permission control, three-tier ecosystem integration spanning MCP, Skills, and Plugins, and a background task framework with separated execution and observation privileges. These mechanisms collectively address the engineering challenges of transforming a complex agent engine into a shared, programmable core. Demonstrating its architectural versatility, the same Sema Core engine simultaneously powers a VSCode extension and a multi-channel messaging gateway, which we name SemaClaw, to unify agent interactions across platforms such as Telegram and Feishu. ### [130] [Evaluating LLM Agents on Automated Software Analysis Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11270)

Abstract: Numerous software analysis tools exist today, yet applying them to diverse open-source projects remains challenging due to environment setup, dependency resolution, and tool configuration. LLM-based agents offer a potential solution, yet no prior work has systematically studied their effectiveness on the specific task of automated software analysis, which, unlike issue solving or general environment setup, requires installing and configuring a separate analysis tool alongside the target project, generating tool-specific prerequisites, and validating that the tool produces meaningful analysis outputs. We introduce AnalysisBench, a benchmark of 35 tool-project pairs spanning seven analysis tools and ten diverse C/C++ and Java projects, each with a manually constructed reference setup. Using AnalysisBench, we evaluate four agent architectures across four LLM backends. Our custom agent, AnalysisAgent, achieves manually verified success rates of 94% (Gemini-3-Flash, 33/35 tasks), compared to 77% for the best baseline (ExecutionAgent). Beyond quantitative results, we identify key limitations in existing agents, including stage mixing, poor error localization, and premature termination, and show that agentic architecture matters more than LLM capability alone. We further find that whole-program analyses and symbolic execution are the most difficult tasks, that Java toolchains pose greater challenges than C/C++, and that LLM-self-validated success consistently overstates manually verified success.

Abstract: This work addresses test output prediction, a key challenge in test case generation. To improve the reliability of predicted outputs by LLMs, prior approaches generate code first to ground predictions. One grounding strategy is direct execution of generated code, but even minor errors can cause failures. To address this, we introduce LLM-based pseudocode execution, which grounds prediction on more error-resilient pseudocode and simulates execution via LLM reasoning. We further propose DuET, a dual-execution framework that combines both approaches by functional majority voting. Our analysis shows the two approaches are complementary in overcoming the limitations of direct execution suffering from code errors, and pseudocode reasoning from hallucination. On LiveCodeBench, DuET achieves the state-of-the-art performance, improving Pass@1 by 13.6 pp.

Result: Python移植版在SWE-bench Verified任务中解决73.8%的任务（Rust为70.0%），在Terminal-Bench上达到42.5%（Rust为47.5%），代码量减少15.9倍，并扩展了30个功能特性。

Conclusion: 对于LLM代理系统，Python的表达能力在API延迟主导的场景下具有优势，基准测试作为目标函数的方法为跨语言移植提供了系统化框架。

Abstract: Cross-language migration of large software systems is a persistent engineering challenge, particularly when the source codebase evolves rapidly. We present a methodology for LLM-assisted continuous code translation in which a large language model translates a production Rust codebase (648K LOC, 65 crates) into Python (41K LOC, 28 modules), with public agent benchmarks as the objective function driving iterative refinement. Our subject system is Codex CLI, a production AI coding agent. We demonstrate that: (1) the Python port resolves 59/80 SWE-bench Verified tasks (73.8%) versus Rust's 56/80 (70.0%), and achieves 42.5% on Terminal-Bench versus Rust's 47.5%, confirming near-parity on real-world agentic tasks; (2) benchmark-driven debugging, revealing API protocol mismatches, environment pollution, a silent WebSocket failure mode, and an API 400 crash, is more effective than static testing alone; (3) the architecture supports continuous upstream synchronisation via an LLM-assisted diff-translate-test loop; and (4) the Python port has evolved into a capability superset with 30 feature-flagged extensions (multi-agent orchestration, semantic memory, guardian safety, cost tracking) absent from Rust, while preserving strict parity mode for comparison. Our evaluation shows that for LLM-based agents where API latency dominates, Python's expressiveness yields a 15.9x code reduction with negligible performance cost, while the benchmark-as-objective-function methodology provides a principled framework for growing a cross-language port from parity into an extended platform.

</details>


### [133] [FM-Agent: Scaling Formal Methods to Large Systems via LLM-Based Hoare-Style Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11556)
*Haoran Ding,Zhaoguo Wang,Haibo Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: FM-Agent：首个实现大规模系统自动组合推理的框架，利用LLM自动生成函数级规范，支持自然语言规范推理，在已测试的大型系统中发现了522个新bug


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM辅助软件开发生成大规模系统时，确保代码正确性至关重要。传统Hoare逻辑需要为每个函数编写形式化规范，人工负担重，尤其当代码由LLM生成时，开发者缺乏对每个函数预期行为的深入理解。

Method: FM-Agent采用自上而下的范式，利用LLM自动生成函数级规范：从调用者对函数的期望行为推导函数规范，即使实现有bug也能反映开发者意图。将Hoare式推理推广到自然语言规范，并自动生成测试用例触发潜在bug。

Result: FM-Agent在2天内成功推理了最多14.3万行代码的大规模系统。在开发者已测试的系统中，仍发现了522个新bug，这些bug可能导致系统崩溃和执行结果错误等严重后果。

Conclusion: FM-Agent是首个实现大规模系统自动组合推理的框架，通过LLM自动生成规范、支持自然语言推理和自动测试生成，有效解决了大规模系统验证的扩展性问题。

Abstract: LLM-assisted software development has become increasingly prevalent, and can generate large-scale systems, such as compilers. It becomes crucial to strengthen the correctness of the generated code. However, automated reasoning for large-scale systems remains challenging due to code complexity. Hoare logic offers an approach to decomposing a large system into smaller components and reasoning about them separately (i.e., compositional reasoning). However, existing works still struggle to scale, because Hoare logic requires writing formal specifications for each function, imposing a heavy human burden. The problem is exacerbated when code is generated by LLMs, as developers lack a deep understanding of each function's expected behavior.
  This paper presents FM-Agent, the first framework that realizes automated compositional reasoning for large-scale systems. Leveraging LLMs, FM-Agent introduces a top-down paradigm to automatically generate function-level specifications. Specifically, FM-Agent derives the specification of a function from how its callers expect the function to behave, so the generated specifications can reflect the developer's intent of a function even if the implementation is buggy. Developers' intent is usually expressed in natural language, while existing verifiers only support formulas. Therefore, FM-Agent generalizes Hoare-style inference to reason about functions against natural-language specifications. Finally, to confirm bug existence and explain bug causes, FM-Agent automatically generates test cases to trigger potential bugs. In our evaluation, FM-Agent successfully reasons about large-scale systems within 2 days, each of which has up to 143k LoC. These systems have already been tested by their developers, but FM-Agent still finds 522 newly discovered bugs. These bugs can cause serious consequences, including system crashes and incorrect execution results.

</details>


### [134] [CodeTracer: Towards Traceable Agent States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.11641)
*Han Li,Yifan Yao,Letian Zhu,Rili Feng,Hongyi Ye,Jiaming Wang,Yancheng He,Pengyu Zou,Lehan Zhang,Xinping Lei,Haoyang Huang,Ken Deng,Ming Sun,Zhaoxiang Zhang,He Ye,Jiaheng Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: CodeTracer是一个追踪架构，用于解析异构运行工件，重建完整状态转换历史作为层次化追踪树，并进行故障起始定位，以精确定位故障起源及其下游链。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着代码代理的快速发展，调试变得越来越困难。框架编排并行工具调用和多阶段工作流，使得代理的状态转换和错误传播难以观察。早期的失误可能导致代理陷入无效率循环或级联成根本性错误，形成隐藏的错误链，难以判断代理何时偏离轨道及原因。

Method: CodeTracer通过演化提取器解析异构运行工件，将完整状态转换历史重建为具有持久内存的层次化追踪树，并执行故障起始定位以精确定位故障起源及其下游链。构建CodeTraceBench用于系统评估，包含四个广泛使用的代码代理框架在多样化代码任务上执行的大量轨迹。

Result: 实验表明，CodeTracer显著优于直接提示和轻量级基线方法，其诊断信号的重放在匹配预算下能持续恢复原本失败的运行。

Conclusion: CodeTracer提供了一个有效的追踪架构，能够解决代码代理调试中的可观察性问题，通过系统化故障定位帮助理解和改进代理行为。

Abstract: Code agents are advancing rapidly, but debugging them is becoming increasingly difficult. As frameworks orchestrate parallel tool calls and multi-stage workflows over complex tasks, making the agent's state transitions and error propagation hard to observe. In these runs, an early misstep can trap the agent in unproductive loops or even cascade into fundamental errors, forming hidden error chains that make it hard to tell when the agent goes off track and why. Existing agent tracing analyses either focus on simple interaction or rely on small-scale manual inspection, which limits their scalability and usefulness for real coding workflows. We present CodeTracer, a tracing architecture that parses heterogeneous run artifacts through evolving extractors, reconstructs the full state transition history as a hierarchical trace tree with persistent memory, and performs failure onset localization to pinpoint the failure origin and its downstream chain. To enable systematic evaluation, we construct CodeTraceBench from a large collection of executed trajectories generated by four widely used code agent frameworks on diverse code tasks (e.g., bug fixing, refactoring, and terminal interaction), with supervision at both the stage and step levels for failure localization. Experiments show that CodeTracer substantially outperforms direct prompting and lightweight baselines, and that replaying its diagnostic signals consistently recovers originally failed runs under matched budgets. Our code and data are publicly available.

</details>

As a result, LLMs should be used as tools to support human judgment and abstraction, not replace it, or they risk increasing system complexity rather than improving it.

### [138] [Selective Test Execution at Stripe: Fast CI for a 50M-line Ruby monorepo](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fstripe.dev%2Fblog%2Fselective-test-execution-at-stripe-fast-ci-for-a-50m-line-ruby-monorepo%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019d86858a32-f61d7ffc-4302-42ef-afeb-3915612517d8-000000/PtrBIiorSkU80vS0Yv-m6PMCPzkZnYBP1rqyuZIMAkE=452)
*TLDR Newsletter*

Main category: tldr.article

TL;DR: Stripe开发了选择性测试执行系统，在5000万行Ruby单体仓库中通过动态追踪文件访问，只运行受代码变更影响的测试子集，从而保持CI快速运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在拥有5000万行代码的庞大Ruby单体仓库中，运行所有测试会导致CI时间过长，影响开发效率。需要一种方法在保持测试安全性的同时显著减少测试执行时间。

Method: 采用选择性测试执行方法，动态追踪测试运行期间的文件访问，建立测试与文件之间的依赖关系图。当代码变更时，只重新运行受影响的测试。同时设置安全护栏，如始终运行关键测试或之前失败的测试。

Result: 该方法避免了不可靠的静态分析，实现了大规模计算节省，在保持测试安全性的同时显著加快了CI速度，使大规模单体仓库的持续集成变得可行。

Conclusion: 选择性测试执行是处理大规模代码库CI挑战的有效解决方案，通过动态依赖追踪和智能测试选择，在保证质量的同时大幅提升开发效率。

Abstract: Selective Test Execution at Stripe: Fast CI for a 50M-line Ruby monorepo (8 minute read) Stripe keeps CI fast in a massive Ruby monorepo by running only a small subset of tests using Selective Test Execution, which dynamically tracks file access during test runs and re-executes only tests affected by code changes. This approach avoids unreliable static analysis, achieves large compute savings, and maintains safety through guardrails like always running critical or previously failing tests.

</details>

### [149] [Agent coordination is emerging as the real bottleneck](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.computerworld.com%2Farticle%2F3843138%2Fagentic-ai-ongoing-coverage-of-its-impact-on-the-enterprise.html%3Futm_source=tldrit/1/0100019d86c3815a-6e95fb4a-fffb-4e38-a22d-4577b09d8a3d-000000/kz1CQ0GtMs8EnvxE5KidaRx8gyron3T2MteIJiGtxqE=452)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多智能体系统在演示阶段表现良好，但在实际生产部署中面临协调、成本控制和治理方面的挑战，这些成为阻碍系统成功应用的关键瓶颈

Method: 文章主要讨论多智能体系统的实际部署问题，而非提出具体技术方法。重点分析生产环境中协调、成本控制和治理的挑战

Result: 识别出多智能体系统从演示到生产部署的主要障碍：协调复杂性、成本控制难度和治理机制缺失
